    function tcAdvInit(params) {
        if (typeof params == 'undefined' || !params.method || !params.divs) {
            console.error('Invalid params for called function');
            return;
        }
        var gWidth = window.innerWidth;

        for (var div in params.divs) {
            var zone = params.divs[div].idZone;
            var adSub = params.adSub;
            var bp = params.divs[div].breakPoint;
            var opts = params.divs[div].opts || null;

            if (typeof ExoLoader !== 'undefined' && adver.isAdblock()) {
                ExoLoader.addZone({
                    type: 'banner',
                    width: '300',
                    height: '250',
                    idzone: zone,
                    "sub": adSub,
                    "container": document.getElementById(div)
                });
            }
            if (bp && gWidth <= bp) continue;
            if (params.method == 'direct' && !adver.isAdblock()) {
                tcDirectSet(div, zone);
            } else if (params.method == 'adver' && !adver.isAdblock()){
                tcAdvertSet(div, opts)
            }
        }
    }

    function tcDirectSet(div, zone) {
        var spot = document.getElementById(div);
        var empty = spot.querySelector('iframe') ? true : false;

        if(empty) return;

        spot.innerHTML = '<iframe frameborder="0" scrolling="no" width="300" height="250" src="' + exoDocumentProtocol + '//syndication.exosrv.com/ads-iframe-display.php?idzone=' + zone + '&type=' + ad_type + '&p=' + escape(p) + '&dt=' + dt + '&sub=' + ad_sub + '&tags=' + ad_tags + '&screen_resolution=' + ad_screen_resolution + '"></iframe>';
    }

    function tcAdvertSet(div, opts) {

        var spot = document.getElementById(div);
        var empty = spot.querySelector('iframe') ? true : false;

        if(empty) return;

        adver.init('banner', opts);
    }
</script>

<script>
    var isIE = detectIE();
    
    (isIE && isIE < 11) && alert('U wot? U use IE version ' + isIE + '? Siriously?')

    if (isIE && isIE === 11) {
        !document.querySelector('.day') && (document.body.style.background = '#202020')
        getScript('/script/feedbackBabel.js?v=3.2', checkReportsCount)
    } 
    else getScript('/script/feedback.js?v=3.2', checkReportsCount)

    
    function detectIE() {
        var ua = window.navigator.userAgent;
        var msie = ua.indexOf('MSIE ');

        // IE 10 or older => return version number
        if (msie > 0)
            return parseInt(ua.substring(msie + 5, ua.indexOf('.', msie)), 10);
        // IE 11 => return version number
        var trident = ua.indexOf('Trident/');
        if (trident > 0) {
            var rv = ua.indexOf('rv:');
            return parseInt(ua.substring(rv + 3, ua.indexOf('.', rv)), 10);
        }

        return false; // other browser
    }
    
    function getScript(source, callback) {
        var script = document.createElement('script');
        var prior = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
        script.async = 1;

        script.onload = script.onreadystatechange = function( _, isAbort ) {
            if(isAbort || !script.readyState || /loaded|complete/.test(script.readyState) ) {
                script.onload = script.onreadystatechange = null;
                script = undefined;

                if(!isAbort) { if(callback) callback(); }
            }
        };

        script.src = source;
        prior.parentNode.insertBefore(script, prior);
    }

    function checkReportsCount () {
        var reportsCount = document.cookie.replace(/(?:(?:^|.*;\s*)report\s*\=\s*([^;]*).*$)|^.*$/, "$1")
        if (reportsCount == 5) {
            !!~location.href.indexOf('form.html') &&
                alert('You have sent too many reports.\nTry again later')
            
            let formSubmitButton = document.querySelector('button[type=submit]')
            formSubmitButton.setAttribute('disabled', true)
            formSubmitButton.style.backgroundColor = '#701B1B'
        }
    }
</script><div class="close-container feedback-close__container"></div></div>

<script>
	let button = document.querySelector('[data-target="#modal-iframe"]'),
		isIE11 = !!navigator.userAgent.match(/Trident\/7\./),
		IEold = ( navigator.userAgent.match(/MSIE/i) ? true : false );

	(!(isIE11 || IEold) && !!button && window.matchMedia("(min-width: 350px)").matches) 
		&& button.addEventListener('click', openReportModal)

	function openReportModal (e) {
		e.preventDefault()
		// check reports count
		var reportsCount = document.cookie.replace(/(?:(?:^|.*;\s*)report\s*\=\s*([^;]*).*$)|^.*$/, "$1")
		if (reportsCount == 5) {
			alert('You have sent too many reports.\nTry again later')
			button.classList.add('report-blocked')
			return
		}
		
		let modal = document.querySelector('.report-modal'),
			closeButton = document.querySelector('.feedback-close__container'),
			modalBg = document.querySelector('.report-modal__bg')
		// show modal
		modal.style.zIndex = 10000
		modal.classList.add('modal-open')
		// show layer behind modal
		modalBg.style.zIndex = 5000
		modalBg.style.opacity = 1
		// remove scrolling when modal is opened
		document.body.style.height = '100%'
		document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden'

		// add close listener on button and area around forma
		for(let elem of [closeButton, modalBg]) {
			elem.addEventListener('click', () => {
				modal.classList.remove('modal-open')
				setTimeout(() => {
					// hide feedback modal
					modal.style.zIndex = -1
					modalBg.style.zIndex = -1
					// return scrolling
					document.body.style.height = ''
					document.body.style.overflow = ''
				}, 300)
				modalBg.style.opacity = 0
			}, {once: true})
		}
	}
</script>
